INNER JOIN [Users] AS [u] ON [a].[UserId] = [u].[Id]
INNER JOIN [Roles] AS [r] ON [u].[RoleId] = [r].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c].[Id], [c].[ArticleId], [c].[CreatedDate], [c].[Text], [c].[UserId], [u0].[Id] AS [Id0], [u0].[About], [u0].[DateOfTheBirth], [u0].[Email], [u0].[FirstName], [u0].[Image], [u0].[Login], [u0].[Password], [u0].[PhoneNumber], [u0].[RememberMe], [u0].[RoleId], [u0].[Status], [u0].[Surname]

) AS [t] ON [a].[Id] = [t].[ArticleId]

ORDER BY [a].[Id], [u].[Id], [r].[Id], [t].[Id], [t].[Id0]

FROM [Articles] AS [a]
INNER JOIN [Users] AS [u] ON [a].[UserId] = [u].[Id]
INNER JOIN [Roles] AS [r] ON [u].[RoleId] = [r].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c].[Id], [c].[ArticleId], [c].[CreatedDate], [c].[Text], [c].[UserId], [u0].[Id] AS [Id0], [u0].[About], [u0].[DateOfTheBirth], [u0].[Email], [u0].[FirstName], [u0].[Image], [u0].[Login], [u0].[Password], [u0].[PhoneNumber], [u0].[RememberMe], [u0].[RoleId], [u0].[Status], [u0].[Surname]

SELECT [a].[Id], [a].[DatePosted], [a].[Description], [a].[Title], [a].[UserId], [u].[Id], [r].[Id], [t].[Id], [t].[ArticleId], [t].[CreatedDate], [t].[Text], [t].[UserId], [t].[Id0], [t].[About], [t].[DateOfTheBirth], [t].[Email], [t].[FirstName], [t].[Image], [t].[Login], [t].[Password], [t].[PhoneNumber], [t].[RememberMe], [t].[RoleId], [t].[Status], [t].[Surname], [u].[About], [u].[DateOfTheBirth], [u].[Email], [u].[FirstName], [u].[Image], [u].[Login], [u].[Password], [u].[PhoneNumber], [u].[RememberMe], [u].[RoleId], [u].[Status], [u].[Surname], [r].[Name], [t0].[Id], [t0].[ArticleId], [t0].[Name]
FROM [Articles] AS [a]
INNER JOIN [Users] AS [u] ON [a].[UserId] = [u].[Id]
INNER JOIN [Roles] AS [r] ON [u].[RoleId] = [r].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c].[Id], [c].[ArticleId], [c].[CreatedDate], [c].[Text], [c].[UserId], [u0].[Id] AS [Id0], [u0].[About], [u0].[DateOfTheBirth], [u0].[Email], [u0].[FirstName], [u0].[Image], [u0].[Login], [u0].[Password], [u0].[PhoneNumber], [u0].[RememberMe], [u0].[RoleId], [u0].[Status], [u0].[Surname]

) AS [t] ON [a].[Id] = [t].[ArticleId]
LEFT JOIN [Tags] AS [t0] ON [a].[Id] = [t0].[ArticleId]
ORDER BY [a].[Id], [u].[Id], [r].[Id], [t].[Id], [t].[Id0]

LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c].[Id], [c].[ArticleId], [c].[CreatedDate], [c].[Text], [c].[UserId], [u0].[Id] AS [Id0], [u0].[About], [u0].[DateOfTheBirth], [u0].[Email], [u0].[FirstName], [u0].[Image], [u0].[Login], [u0].[Password], [u0].[PhoneNumber], [u0].[RememberMe], [u0].[RoleId], [u0].[Status], [u0].[Surname]

    SELECT TOP(1) [a].[Id], [a].[DatePosted], [a].[Description], [a].[Title], [a].[UserId], [u].[Id] AS [Id0], [u].[About], [u].[DateOfTheBirth], [u].[Email], [u].[FirstName], [u].[Image], [u].[Login], [u].[Password], [u].[PhoneNumber], [u].[RememberMe], [u].[RoleId], [u].[Status], [u].[Surname], [r].[Id] AS [Id1], [r].[Name]
    FROM [Articles] AS [a]
    INNER JOIN [Users] AS [u] ON [a].[UserId] = [u].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [Roles] AS [r] ON [u].[RoleId] = [r].[Id]
    WHERE [a].[Id] = @__id_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c].[Id], [c].[ArticleId], [c].[CreatedDate], [c].[Text], [c].[UserId], [u0].[Id] AS [Id0], [u0].[About], [u0].[DateOfTheBirth], [u0].[Email], [u0].[FirstName], [u0].[Image], [u0].[Login], [u0].[Password], [u0].[PhoneNumber], [u0].[RememberMe], [u0].[RoleId], [u0].[Status], [u0].[Surname]
    FROM [Comments] AS [c]
    INNER JOIN [Users] AS [u0] ON [c].[UserId] = [u0].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[ArticleId]
LEFT JOIN [Tags] AS [t1] ON [t].[Id] = [t1].[ArticleId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [t].[Id0], [t].[Id1], [t0].[Id], [t0].[Id0]

INNER JOIN [Roles] AS [r] ON [u].[RoleId] = [r].[Id]

    SELECT [c].[Id], [c].[ArticleId], [c].[CreatedDate], [c].[Text], [c].[UserId], [u0].[Id] AS [Id0], [u0].[About], [u0].[DateOfTheBirth], [u0].[Email], [u0].[FirstName], [u0].[Image], [u0].[Login], [u0].[Password], [u0].[PhoneNumber], [u0].[RememberMe], [u0].[RoleId], [u0].[Status], [u0].[Surname]
